    <script type="text/javascript">
     jQuery(".aboopenclose").on("click", function () {
	if (clRecmnd_state == "disabled") return false;
	if (jQuery(".clRecmnd .abocontent").height() == 0) {
		jQuery(".clRecmnd .abocontent").animate({
			"height": "196px"
		}, 400);
		jQuery(".aboopenclose").attr("src", "/i/6/rcmnaboupbut.png");
		jQuery(".aboopenclose").addClass("aboopenclose2");
	} else {
		jQuery(".clRecmnd .abocontent").animate({
			"height": "0px"
		}, 400);
		jQuery(".aboopenclose").removeClass("aboopenclose2");
	}
});
clRecmnd_state = "inactive";
clRecmnd_anim = 0;
clRecmnd_t = 0;
clRecmnd_first = true;
clRecmnd_cookie = readCookie("clRecmnd_cookie");
showAboKare = true;
if (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/light/') === 0 &amp;&amp; ((new Date()).getTime() &lt; (new Date(2014, 1, 6, 0, 0, 0, 0)).getTime())) {
	showAboKare = false;
}

showAboKare = false;

if (!showAboKare || clRecmnd_cookie == 1) {
	jQuery(".clRecmnd .abocontent").css("height", "0px");
	jQuery(".clRecmnd .abocontent,.clRecmnd .abohead, .clRecmnd .aboheaddlysh").css("display", "none");
	clRecmnd_first = false;
} else {
	createCookie("clRecmnd_cookie", 1, 1);
	jQuery(".clRecmnd .head, .clRecmnd a, .clRecmnd p").css("display", "none");
}
jQuery(window).scroll(function () {
	if (clRecmnd_state == "disabled") return false;
	if (jQuery("#endofstory").offset().top &gt; 0 == 0) return false;
	if (clRecmnd_anim == 1) return false;
	var wScroll = jQuery(window).scrollTop() + jQuery(window).height();
	var eTop = jQuery("#endofstory").offset().top - 100;
	
	if (clRecmnd_state == "inactive") {
		if ( eTop &lt; wScroll ) {
			if (clRecmnd_first) {
				clRecmnd_first = false;
				clRecmnd_t = setTimeout("jQuery('.aboopenclose').click();",5000);
			}
			clRecmnd_anim = 1;
			clRecmnd_state = "active";
			jQuery(".clRecmnd:first").animate({
				marginRight: "0px"
			}, 800, function() {
				clRecmnd_anim = 0;
			});
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}
	if (clRecmnd_state == "active") {
		if ( eTop &gt; wScroll ) {
			clRecmnd_anim = 1;
			clRecmnd_state = "inactive";
			jQuery(".clRecmnd:first").animate({
				marginRight: "-400px"
			}, 800, function() {
				clRecmnd_anim = 0;
			});
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}
});
    </script>
